                console.log('1?¨ê³„ ?€?´ë¨¸ ?ë™ ?œì‘');
            }
        }

// ?¼â–¼???¸í„°?™í‹°ë¸??°ëª¨ ?¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ (High-Fidelity) ?¼â–¼??
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const guideBtn = document.getElementById('demoGuideBtn');
    const exampleBtn = document.getElementById('demoExampleBtn');
    const keywordBtn = document.getElementById('demoKeywordBtn');
    
    const guideContainer = document.getElementById('demoGuideContainer');
    const exampleContainer = document.getElementById('demoExampleContainer');
    const keywordModal = document.getElementById('demoKeywordModal');

    // ê³µí†µ ? ê? ?¨ìˆ˜
    function toggleDemoContainer(containerToShow) {
        const allContainers = [guideContainer, exampleContainer];
        
        allContainers.forEach(container => {
            if (container === containerToShow) {
                container.classList.toggle('visible'); // ?´ë¦­??ê±?? ê?
            } else {
                container.classList.remove('visible'); // ?˜ë¨¸ì§??«ê¸°
            }
        });
    }

    // ë²„íŠ¼ ?´ë¦­ ?´ë²¤???¤ì •
    if(guideBtn) guideBtn.addEventListener('click', () => toggleDemoContainer(guideContainer));
    if(exampleBtn) exampleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => toggleDemoContainer(exampleContainer));
    if(keywordBtn) keywordBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if(keywordModal) keywordModal.style.display = 'block';
    });
});

// ?°ëª¨ ëª¨ë‹¬ ?«ê¸°
function closeDemoModal(modalId) {
    const modal = document.getElementById(modalId);
    if(modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
}

// ?°ëª¨ ?¤ì›Œ??ì¶”ê?/?? œ
function addDemoKeyword(keyword) {
    const tagsContainer = document.getElementById('demoKeywordsTags');
    if (!tagsContainer) return;
    
    const noKeywordsSpan = tagsContainer.querySelector('.no-keywords');
    if (noKeywordsSpan) noKeywordsSpan.style.display = 'none';
    
    if (document.getElementById(`demo-tag-${keyword}`)) {
        closeDemoModal('demoKeywordModal');
        return;
    }

    const newTag = document.createElement('span');
    newTag.className = 'keyword-tag';
    newTag.id = `demo-tag-${keyword}`;
    newTag.textContent = keyword;
    
    const removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
    removeBtn.className = 'remove-btn';
    removeBtn.innerHTML = '&times;';
    removeBtn.onclick = () => {
        newTag.remove();
        if (tagsContainer.querySelectorAll('.keyword-tag').length === 0) {
             if (noKeywordsSpan) noKeywordsSpan.style.display = 'inline';
        }
    };
    
    newTag.appendChild(removeBtn);
    tagsContainer.appendChild(newTag);
    closeDemoModal('demoKeywordModal');
}

let completeStage3Questions = null; // ëª¨ë“  ?•ë³´ê°€ ?µí•©??3?¨ê³„ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´???€?¥ìš©
let stage3SelectedQuestionIds = null; // 3?¨ê³„ ???˜ì´ì§€??ë³´ì—¬ì¤?ì§ˆë¬¸ ID ?€?¥ìš©


function combineQuestionData(originalQuestions, newCategoryInfoArray) {
    return originalQuestions.map(originalQ => {
        const matchingInfo = newCategoryInfoArray.find(info => info.id === originalQ.id);
        if (matchingInfo) {
            return {
                ...originalQ,
                reflectionCategory: matchingInfo.reflectionCategory,
                attractionCategories: matchingInfo.attractionCategories
            };
        } else {
            console.warn(`[combineQuestionData] ì£¼ì˜: ID ${originalQ.id}???€??ì¶”ê? ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ?•ë³´ë¥?newStage3CategoryInfo ë°°ì—´?ì„œ ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.`);
            return originalQ;
        }
    });
}

// testlogic.js ?Œì¼??ì¶”ê??˜ì„¸??
// (newStage3CategoryInfo, completeStage3Questions, userAttractionScores ë³€?˜ê?
//  ???¨ìˆ˜ë¥??¸ì¶œ?˜ëŠ” ?œì ?ëŠ” ì¤€ë¹„ë˜???ˆì–´???©ë‹ˆ??)

/**
 * 1, 2?¨ê³„ ?‘ë‹µ??ê¸°ë°˜?¼ë¡œ 3?¨ê³„???œì‹œ??ê°œì¸?”ëœ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?©ì–´ë¦?ID ??ê°œë? ? íƒ?©ë‹ˆ??
 * ? íƒ????ì§ˆë¬¸?€ ?œë¡œ ?¤ë¥¸ ?±ì°° ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬???í•´???©ë‹ˆ??
 *
 * @param {Array<Object>} allAugmentedQuestions - ëª¨ë“  ?•ë³´ê°€ ?µí•©??3?¨ê³„ ì§ˆë¬¸ ê°ì²´ ë°°ì—´ (completeStage3Questions).
 * ê°?ê°ì²´??id, reflectionCategory, attractionCategories, ... ?±ì„ ?¬í•¨.
 * @param {Object} userScores - ?¬ìš©?ì˜ 7ê°€ì§€ ë§¤ë ¥ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ë³??ìˆ˜ ê°ì²´.
 * @returns {Object|null} { firstQuestionId: id1, secondQuestionId: id2 } ?•íƒœ??ê°ì²´, ?ëŠ” ?¤íŒ¨ ??null.
 */
function selectPersonalizedStage3Questions(allAugmentedQuestions, userScores) {
    // [ê²€ì¦? ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´?°ê? 3ê°?ë¯¸ë§Œ?´ë©´ ê°œì¸??? íƒ??ë¶ˆê??¥í•©?ˆë‹¤.
    if (!allAugmentedQuestions || allAugmentedQuestions.length < 3) {
        console.error("[selectPersonalizedStage3Questions] ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´?°ê? 3ê°?ë¯¸ë§Œ?´ë¼ ê°œì¸??? íƒ??ë¶ˆê??¥í•©?ˆë‹¤.");
        return null;
    }
    // [ê²€ì¦? ?¬ìš©???ìˆ˜ ?°ì´?°ê? ?†ìœ¼ë©?ë¬´ì‘?„ë¡œ 3ê°œë? ? íƒ?©ë‹ˆ??
    if (!userScores) {
        console.warn("[selectPersonalizedStage3Questions] ?¬ìš©???ìˆ˜ ?°ì´?°ê? ?†ì–´ ë¬´ì‘??? íƒ?©ë‹ˆ??");
        const shuffled = allAugmentedQuestions.sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
        return { firstQuestionId: shuffled[0].id, secondQuestionId: shuffled[1].id, thirdQuestionId: shuffled[2].id };
    }

    // 1. ê°?ì§ˆë¬¸??'ê°œì¸???í•©???ìˆ˜' ê³„ì‚°
    const questionsWithFitness = allAugmentedQuestions.map(qg => {
        let qgFitnessScore = qg.attractionCategories.reduce((score, acName) => score + (userScores[acName] || 0), 0);
        return { ...qg, qgFitnessScore };
    });

    // 2. 4ê°€ì§€ '?±ì°° ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬'ë³?ì´??ìˆ˜ ë°?ì§ˆë¬¸ ëª©ë¡ ê³„ì‚°
    const rcScores = { "ê²½í—˜": 0, "ê°€ì¹?: 0, "?±ì¥": 0, "ê´€ê³?: 0 };
    const questionsByRC = { "ê²½í—˜": [], "ê°€ì¹?: [], "?±ì¥": [], "ê´€ê³?: [] };

    questionsWithFitness.forEach(qg => {
        if (rcScores.hasOwnProperty(qg.reflectionCategory)) {
            rcScores[qg.reflectionCategory] += qg.qgFitnessScore;
            questionsByRC[qg.reflectionCategory].push(qg);
        }
    });

    // 3. ?ìˆ˜ ?œìœ¼ë¡??±ì°° ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ?•ë ¬
    const sortedRC = Object.entries(rcScores)
        .map(([name, score]) => ({ name, score, questions: questionsByRC[name] }))
        .filter(rc => rc.questions.length > 0)
        .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);

    // 4. ìµœì¢… ? íƒ??ì§ˆë¬¸ ID?¤ì„ ?€?¥í•  Set (ì¤‘ë³µ ë°©ì?)
    const selectedIds = new Set();
    
    // ?±ì°° ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ?´ì—??ìµœê³ ??ì§ˆë¬¸??ì°¾ëŠ” ?¨ìˆ˜
    const findBestQuestionIdInRC = (rcObject) => {
        if (!rcObject || rcObject.questions.length === 0) return null;
        rcObject.questions.sort((a, b) => b.qgFitnessScore - a.qgFitnessScore);
        for (const question of rcObject.questions) {
            if (!selectedIds.has(question.id)) return question.id;
        }
        return null;
    };

    // 5. ?ìœ„ 3ê°?ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬?ì„œ ê°ê° ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ ?œë„
    sortedRC.slice(0, 3).forEach(rc => {
        const bestId = findBestQuestionIdInRC(rc);
        if (bestId) selectedIds.add(bestId);
    });
    
    // 6. [?€ì²?ë¡œì§] ë§Œì•½ 3ê°œê? ? íƒ?˜ì? ?Šì•˜?¤ë©´, ?„ì²´ ì§ˆë¬¸ ëª©ë¡?ì„œ ?í•©???œìœ¼ë¡?ë¶€ì¡±í•œ ë§Œí¼ ì±„ìš°ê¸?    if (selectedIds.size < 3) {
        questionsWithFitness.sort((a, b) => b.qgFitnessScore - a.qgFitnessScore);
        for (const question of questionsWithFitness) {
            if (selectedIds.size >= 3) break;
            selectedIds.add(question.id);
        }
    }
    
    // 7. ìµœì¢… ê²°ê³¼ ë°˜í™˜
    const [firstQuestionId, secondQuestionId, thirdQuestionId] = Array.from(selectedIds);

    if (firstQuestionId && secondQuestionId && thirdQuestionId) {
        return { firstQuestionId, secondQuestionId, thirdQuestionId };
    } else {
        // [ìµœí›„???€ì²?ë¡œì§] ê·¸ë˜???¤íŒ¨ ?? ë¬´ì‘??3ê°?ë°˜í™˜
        console.error("3ê°œì˜ ê°œì¸??ì§ˆë¬¸??? íƒ?˜ëŠ” ???¤íŒ¨?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. ê¸°ë³¸ ì§ˆë¬¸ 3ê°œë? ë°˜í™˜?©ë‹ˆ??");
        const shuffled = allAugmentedQuestions.sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
        return { firstQuestionId: shuffled[0].id, secondQuestionId: shuffled[1].id, thirdQuestionId: shuffled[2].id };
    }
}
// testlogic.js ?Œì¼ ?ë‹¨ ?ëŠ” ?ì ˆ???„ì¹˜??ì¶”ê?
const ALL_PERSONALITY_QUESTIONS_POOL = [
    {
        id: 'per_q1',
        text: "?˜ì˜ ?ë„ˆì§€ ë°©í–¥?€?",

let stageTimers = {
    stage1Start: null,
    stage2Start: null, 
    stage3Start: null,
    currentPageStart: null
};

let completeTestData = {
    userId: null,
    timestamp: null,
    stage1_selections: [],
    stage2_situation_responses: [],
    stage2_personality_responses: [],
    stage3_responses: {},
    survey_responses: {},
    completed: false,
    stage1_duration: null,
    stage2_duration: null,
    stage3_duration: null

window.stageTimers = stageTimers;

// ?œê°„ ê¸°ë¡ ?¨ìˆ˜??function startStage1Timer() {
    stageTimers.stage1Start = Date.now();
    completeTestData.stage1_duration = null; // ì´ˆê¸°??    console.log('?•’ 1?¨ê³„ ?€?´ë¨¸ ?œì‘:', new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
}

function startStage2Timer() {
    // 1?¨ê³„ ?„ë£Œ ?œê°„ ê³„ì‚°
    if (stageTimers.stage1Start) {
        const stage1Duration = (Date.now() - stageTimers.stage1Start) / 1000;
        completeTestData.stage1_duration = stage1Duration;
        console.log(`??1?¨ê³„ ?„ë£Œ: ${stage1Duration.toFixed(1)}ì´?);
    }
    
    stageTimers.stage2Start = Date.now();
    completeTestData.stage2_duration = null; // ì´ˆê¸°??    console.log('?•’ 2?¨ê³„ ?€?´ë¨¸ ?œì‘:', new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
}

function startStage3Timer() {
    // 2?¨ê³„ ?„ë£Œ ?œê°„ ê³„ì‚°
    if (stageTimers.stage2Start) {
        const stage2Duration = (Date.now() - stageTimers.stage2Start) / 1000;
        completeTestData.stage2_duration = stage2Duration;
        console.log(`??2?¨ê³„ ?„ë£Œ: ${stage2Duration.toFixed(1)}ì´?);
    }
    
    stageTimers.stage3Start = Date.now();
    completeTestData.stage3_duration = null; // ì´ˆê¸°??    console.log('?•’ 3?¨ê³„ ?€?´ë¨¸ ?œì‘:', new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
}

function completeStage3Timer() {
    // 3?¨ê³„ ?„ë£Œ ?œê°„ ê³„ì‚°
    if (stageTimers.stage3Start) {
        const stage3Duration = (Date.now() - stageTimers.stage3Start) / 1000;
        completeTestData.stage3_duration = stage3Duration;
        console.log(`??3?¨ê³„ ?„ë£Œ: ${stage3Duration.toFixed(1)}ì´?);
    }
}

// ê¸°ì¡´ testlogic.js ì½”ë“œ???¬ê¸°ë¶€???œì‘...

class AttractionTestSystem {
    constructor() {
        this.stage1_selections = [];
        this.stage2_situation_responses = [];
        this.stage2_personality_responses = [];
        this.stage3_responses = [];
        this.currentTemplateQuestion = null;
        this.currentTemplateSubIndex = null; // ì¶”ê?: ?œë¸Œ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?¸ë±??        this.attractionCategories = [
            "?´í•´??ë°?ê³µê° ?¥ë ¥",
            "?±ì‹¤??ë°?ì±…ì„ê°?, 
            "ì§€???¸ê¸°??ë°?ê°œë°©??,
            "?•ì„œ???ˆì • ë°??ê¸° ?¸ì‹",
            "?„ë•??ë°??‘ì‹¬",
            "? ë¨¸ê°ê° ë°??¬êµ??,
            "ëª©í‘œ ì§€?¥ì„± ë°??¼ë§"
        ];
        this.allSituationQuestions = this.loadAllSituationQuestions();
         this.allPersonalityQuestions = ALL_PERSONALITY_QUESTIONS_POOL;
    
        
        this.initializeEventListeners();
    }
    
    initializeEventListeners() {
        // 1?¨ê³„ ì²´í¬ë°•ìŠ¤ ?´ë²¤??        document.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            if (e.target.type === 'checkbox' && e.target.closest('#categorySelection')) {
                this.handleCategorySelection();
            }
        });
        
        // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ë°•ìŠ¤ ?´ë¦­ ?´ë²¤??(ë°•ìŠ¤ ?„ì²´ ?´ë¦­ ê°€??
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest('.category-item')) {
                const item = e.target.closest('.category-item');
                const checkbox = item.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
                if (e.target !== checkbox) {
                    checkbox.checked = !checkbox.checked;
                    this.handleCategorySelection();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    handleCategorySelection() {
        const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('#categorySelection input[type="checkbox"]');
        const checkedBoxes = Array.from(checkboxes).filter(cb => cb.checked);
        const stage1Btn = document.getElementById('stage1Btn');
        const errorMsg = document.getElementById('stage1Error');
        
        // ? íƒ????ª©?¤ì˜ ?¤í????…ë°?´íŠ¸
        checkboxes.forEach(cb => {
            const item = cb.closest('.category-item');
            if (cb.checked) {
                item.classList.add('selected');
            } else {
                item.classList.remove('selected');
            }
        });
        
        // 3ê°?ì´ˆê³¼ ? íƒ ë°©ì?
        if (checkedBoxes.length > 3) {
            const lastChecked = checkedBoxes[checkedBoxes.length - 1];
            lastChecked.checked = false;
            lastChecked.closest('.category-item').classList.remove('selected');
            
            errorMsg.textContent = 'ìµœë? 3ê°œê¹Œì§€ë§?? íƒ?????ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.';
            errorMsg.style.display = 'block';
            setTimeout(() => {
                errorMsg.style.display = 'none';
            }, 2000);
            return;
        }
        
        // ? íš¨??ê²€??        if (checkedBoxes.length === 0) {
            stage1Btn.disabled = true;
            errorMsg.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
            stage1Btn.disabled = false;
            errorMsg.style.display = 'none';
        }
    };

// testlogic.js - AttractionTestSystem ?´ë˜???´ë???ì¶”ê?
// ?? getAttractionKeywords() ë©”ì†Œ???¤ìŒ?´ë‚˜, ?´ë˜??ë§?ë§ˆì?ë§‰ì— ì¶”ê?

calculateUserCategoryScores() {
    const scores = {
        "?´í•´??ë°?ê³µê° ?¥ë ¥": 0,
        "?±ì‹¤??ë°?ì±…ì„ê°?: 0,
        "ì§€???¸ê¸°??ë°?ê°œë°©??: 0,
        "?•ì„œ???ˆì • ë°??ê¸° ?¸ì‹": 0,
        "?„ë•??ë°??‘ì‹¬": 0,
        "? ë¨¸ê°ê° ë°??¬êµ??: 0,
        "ëª©í‘œ ì§€?¥ì„± ë°??¼ë§": 0
    };

    // 1?¨ê³„ ? íƒ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬???ìˆ˜ ë¶€??(?? ê°?2??
    this.stage1_selections.forEach(category => {
        if (scores.hasOwnProperty(category)) {
            scores[category] += 2;
        }
    });

    // 2?¨ê³„ ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?‘ë‹µ?ì„œ ? íƒ??? ì???ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬???ìˆ˜ ë¶€??(?? ê°?1??
    this.stage2_situation_responses.forEach(response => {
        if (response.selectedChoice && response.selectedChoice.category) {
            const category = response.selectedChoice.category;
            if (scores.hasOwnProperty(category)) {
                scores[category] += 1;
            }
        }
    });

    console.log("?“Š ?¬ìš©??ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ? í˜¸???ìˆ˜:", scores); // ?•ì¸??ë¡œê·¸
    return scores;
}

// testlogic.js - AttractionTestSystem ?´ë˜???´ë???ì¶”ê?
// ?? calculateUserCategoryScores() ë©”ì†Œ???¤ìŒ?´ë‚˜, ?´ë˜??ë§?ë§ˆì?ë§‰ì— ì¶”ê?

// ê¸°ì¡´ ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥?ì§€?°ê³  ??ì½”ë“œë¡??„ì²´ë¥?êµì²´?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.
getPersonalizedPersonalityQuestions() {
    const userCategoryScores = this.calculateUserCategoryScores();

    const scoredQuestions = this.allPersonalityQuestions.map(question => {
        let relevanceScore = 0;
        if (question.choices.A && userCategoryScores.hasOwnProperty(question.choices.A.category)) {
            relevanceScore += userCategoryScores[question.choices.A.category];
        }
        if (question.choices.B && userCategoryScores.hasOwnProperty(question.choices.B.category)) {
            relevanceScore += userCategoryScores[question.choices.B.category];
        }
        return {
            ...question,
            relevanceScore: relevanceScore
        };
    });

    scoredQuestions.sort((a, b) => b.relevanceScore - a.relevanceScore);

    // ? ï¸ ?˜ì • ?¬ì¸??1: ?ìœ„ 8ê°œì˜ ì§ˆë¬¸??? íƒ?˜ë„ë¡?ë³€ê²?    const topQuestions = scoredQuestions.slice(0, 8);

    let finalSelectedQuestions;

    // ? ï¸ ?˜ì • ?¬ì¸??2: ?„ì²´ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?˜ê? 8ê°œë? ì´ˆê³¼?˜ëŠ”ì§€ ?•ì¸?˜ë„ë¡?ë³€ê²?    if (topQuestions.every(q => q.relevanceScore === 0) && scoredQuestions.length > 8) {
        // ? ï¸ ?˜ì • ?¬ì¸??3: ë¡œê·¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€ ë³€ê²?        console.log("ëª¨ë“  ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸??ê´€?¨ì„± ?ìˆ˜ê°€ 0?´ë?ë¡? ë¬´ì‘?„ë¡œ 8ê°œë? ? íƒ?©ë‹ˆ??");
        const shuffledAll = [...this.allPersonalityQuestions].sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
        // ? ï¸ ?˜ì • ?¬ì¸??4: ë¬´ì‘??? íƒ ?œì—??8ê°œë? ? íƒ?˜ë„ë¡?ë³€ê²?        finalSelectedQuestions = shuffledAll.slice(0, 8);
    } else {
        finalSelectedQuestions = topQuestions;
    }

    // ? ï¸ ?˜ì • ?¬ì¸??5: ìµœì¢… ë¡œê·¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€ ë³€ê²?    console.log("ìµœì¢… ? íƒ??8ê°??±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸:", finalSelectedQuestions);

    this.currentPersonalityQuestions = finalSelectedQuestions;

    return finalSelectedQuestions;
}
}

// ?„ì—­ ?¸ìŠ¤?´ìŠ¤
const testSystem = new AttractionTestSystem();

// ==================== 1?¨ê³„ ??2A?¨ê³„ ====================
function proceedToStage2Situation() {
    // ?•’ 1?¨ê³„ ?€?´ë¨¸ ì¢…ë£Œ ë°?2?¨ê³„ ?€?´ë¨¸ ?œì‘
    startStage2Timer();
    
    const checkedBoxes = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#categorySelection input[type="checkbox"]:checked'));
    testSystem.stage1_selections = checkedBoxes.map(cb => cb.value);
    
   

    // ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?Œë”ë§?    renderSituationQuestions();
    
    // ?”ë©´ ?„í™˜
    document.getElementById('stage1').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('stage2Situation').style.display = 'block';
}

// testlogic.js - ??ì½”ë“œë¡?ê¸°ì¡´ renderSituationQuestions ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??„ì „???€ì²´í•©?ˆë‹¤.

function renderSituationQuestions() { // <--- ?¬ê¸°?œë???ë³µì‚¬ ?œì‘
    const container = document.getElementById('situationQuestionsContainer');
    container.innerHTML = ''; // ê¸°ì¡´ ?´ìš© ì´ˆê¸°??
    // 1. ?„ì²´ ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?€?ì„œ 4ê°œì˜ ì§ˆë¬¸??ë¬´ì‘?„ë¡œ ? íƒ
    const fullQuestionPool = testSystem.allSituationQuestions; 
    
    if (!fullQuestionPool || fullQuestionPool.length === 0) {
        console.error("?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?€(allSituationQuestions)??ë¹„ì–´?ˆê±°???•ì˜?˜ì? ?Šì•˜?µë‹ˆ??");
        container.innerHTML = "<p>?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸??ë¶ˆëŸ¬?¤ëŠ” ???¤íŒ¨?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. ê´€ë¦¬ì?ê²Œ ë¬¸ì˜?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.</p>";
        return;
    }

    const shuffledPool = [...fullQuestionPool].sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
    const selectedQuestionsForStage = shuffledPool.slice(0, 5);

    testSystem.currentStage2SituationQuestions = selectedQuestionsForStage; 

    const userStage1Selections = testSystem.stage1_selections;

    selectedQuestionsForStage.forEach((questionData, questionIndex) => {
        const questionId = questionData.id;
        const questionText = questionData.text;
        const potentialChoices = [...questionData.fullChoices]; 

        let personalizedChoices = [];

        // 3a. 1?¨ê³„?ì„œ ? íƒ??ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬?€ ?¼ì¹˜?˜ëŠ” ? ì? ?°ì„  ì¶”ê?
        userStage1Selections.forEach(selectedCategory => {
            if (personalizedChoices.length >= 4) return;

            const matchedChoiceIndex = potentialChoices.findIndex(choice => choice.category === selectedCategory);
            if (matchedChoiceIndex !== -1) {
                personalizedChoices.push(potentialChoices.splice(matchedChoiceIndex, 1)[0]);
            }
        });

        // 3b. ë¶€ì¡±í•œ ? ì?ë¥??œë¤?¼ë¡œ ì¶”ê?
        let remainingChoices = potentialChoices.filter(pc => 
            !personalizedChoices.some(sc => sc.text === pc.text)
        );

        while (personalizedChoices.length < 4 && remainingChoices.length > 0) {
            const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * remainingChoices.length);
            personalizedChoices.push(remainingChoices.splice(randomIndex, 1)[0]);
        }
        
        const finalChoicesForDisplay = personalizedChoices.map((choice, index) => ({
            letter: String.fromCharCode(65 + index),
            text: choice.text,
            category: choice.category,
            originalChoiceId: choice.choiceId || `choice_${questionId}_${index}` 
        }));

        const questionDiv = document.createElement('div');
        questionDiv.className = 'question-card';
        questionDiv.innerHTML = `
            <div class="question-title">
                ì§ˆë¬¸ ${questionIndex + 1}. ${questionText}
            </div>
            <div class="choices">
                ${finalChoicesForDisplay.map(choice => `
                    <div class="choice-item" onclick="selectChoice('situation', '${questionId}', '${choice.letter}', this)">
                        <input type="radio" name="question_${questionId}" value="${choice.letter}" 
                               data-original-choice-id="${choice.originalChoiceId}" 
                               data-choice-text="${choice.text.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}"
                               data-choice-category="${choice.category}">
                        <div>
                            <strong>${choice.letter}.</strong> ${choice.text}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `).join('')}
            </div>
        `;
        container.appendChild(questionDiv);
    }); 

    checkSituationCompletion();
} // <--- ?¬ê¸°ê¹Œì? ë³µì‚¬?´ì„œ ë¶™ì—¬?£ê¸°

// ==================== 2A?¨ê³„ ??2B?¨ê³„ ====================
function proceedToStage2Personality() {
    
    
    // ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?‘ë‹µ ?˜ì§‘
   // testlogic.js - proceedToStage2Personality ?¨ìˆ˜ ?´ë?ë¥??„ë˜?€ ê°™ì´ ?˜ì •?©ë‹ˆ??

// ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?‘ë‹µ ?˜ì§‘
const responses = [];
// ?´ì „ renderSituationQuestions ?¨ìˆ˜?ì„œ testSystem ê°ì²´???€?¥í•´??// '?„ì¬ ?¬ìš©?ì—ê²?ë³´ì—¬ì§? ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ëª©ë¡???¬ìš©?©ë‹ˆ??
const questionsForStage = testSystem.currentStage2SituationQuestions || []; 

questionsForStage.forEach(questionData => { // questionData??{id, text, fullChoices} ?±ì˜ ?ì„±??ê°€ì§‘ë‹ˆ??
    const questionId = questionData.id; // ?„ì¬ ì§ˆë¬¸??ê³ ìœ  ID
    const selectedRadio = document.querySelector(`input[name="question_${questionId}"]:checked`);

    if (selectedRadio) {
        const choiceLetter = selectedRadio.value;
        // HTML??data-* ?ì„±?ì„œ ? íƒ??? ì????ì„¸ ?•ë³´ë¥?ê°€?¸ì˜µ?ˆë‹¤.
        const choiceText = selectedRadio.dataset.choiceText; 
        const choiceCategory = selectedRadio.dataset.choiceCategory;
        const originalChoiceId = selectedRadio.dataset.originalChoiceId;

        responses.push({
            questionId: questionId,
            questionText: questionData.text, // ?ë³¸ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?ìŠ¤??            selectedChoice: { // ? íƒ??? ì????ì„¸ ?•ë³´
                letter: choiceLetter,
                text: choiceText,
                category: choiceCategory, // ?´ë–¤ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬?€ ?°ê???? ì??¸ì?
                originalChoiceId: originalChoiceId // ?ë³¸ 7ê°?? ì? ì¤??´ë–¤ ê²ƒì´?ˆëŠ”ì§€ ID
            }
        });
    }
});

testSystem.stage2_situation_responses = responses;
console.log("ê°œì¸?”ëœ ?í™© ì§ˆë¬¸ ?‘ë‹µ ?˜ì§‘ ?„ë£Œ: ", testSystem.stage2_situation_responses); // ?•ì¸??ë¡œê·¸



// ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?Œë”ë§?renderPersonalityQuestions();

// ?”ë©´ ?„í™˜
document.getElementById('stage2Situation').style.display = 'none';
document.getElementById('stage2Personality').style.display = 'block';
}

// testlogic.js - renderPersonalityQuestions ?¨ìˆ˜ ?„ì²´ë¥??„ë˜ ?´ìš©?¼ë¡œ êµ¬ì„±?©ë‹ˆ??

function renderPersonalityQuestions() {
    const container = document.getElementById('personalityQuestionsContainer');
    container.innerHTML = ''; // ê¸°ì¡´ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?´ìš©???ˆë‹¤ë©?ëª¨ë‘ ì§€?ë‹ˆ??

    // 3?¨ê³„?ì„œ ë§Œë“  ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??¸ì¶œ?˜ì—¬ ê°œì¸?”ëœ 4ê°œì˜ ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸??ê°€?¸ì˜µ?ˆë‹¤.
    const personalizedQuestions = testSystem.getPersonalizedPersonalityQuestions(); 

    if (!personalizedQuestions || personalizedQuestions.length === 0) {
        console.error("ê°œì¸?”ëœ ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸??ê°€?¸ì˜¤ì§€ ëª»í–ˆ?µë‹ˆ??");
        container.innerHTML = "<p>?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸??ë¶ˆëŸ¬?¤ëŠ” ???¤íŒ¨?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. ê´€ë¦¬ì?ê²Œ ë¬¸ì˜?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.</p>";
        // ë²„íŠ¼ ë¹„í™œ?±í™” ì²˜ë¦¬??ê³ ë ¤?????ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.
        const btn = document.getElementById('stage2PersonalityBtn');
        if (btn) {
            btn.disabled = true;
        }
        return;
    }

    personalizedQuestions.forEach((questionData, index) => {
        const questionId = questionData.id; // ê°?ì§ˆë¬¸??ê³ ìœ  ID (?? 'per_q1')
        const questionText = questionData.text; // ì§ˆë¬¸ ?´ìš©
        // ê°?ì§ˆë¬¸(questionData) ê°ì²´??choices: { A: {text, category}, B: {text, category} } êµ¬ì¡°ë¥?ê°€ì§‘ë‹ˆ??
        const choiceA = questionData.choices.A;
        const choiceB = questionData.choices.B;

        const questionDiv = document.createElement('div');
        questionDiv.className = 'question-card';
        questionDiv.innerHTML = `
            <div class="question-title">
                ì§ˆë¬¸ ${index + 1}. ${questionText}
            </div>
            <div class="choices">
                <div class="choice-item" onclick="selectChoice('personality', '${questionId}', 'A', this)">
                    <input type="radio" name="question_${questionId}" value="A"
                           data-choice-text="${choiceA.text.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}"
                           data-choice-category="${choiceA.category}">
                    <div>
                        <strong>A.</strong> ${choiceA.text}
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="choice-item" onclick="selectChoice('personality', '${questionId}', 'B', this)">
                    <input type="radio" name="question_${questionId}" value="B"
                           data-choice-text="${choiceB.text.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}"
                           data-choice-category="${choiceB.category}">
                    <div>
                        <strong>B.</strong> ${choiceB.text}
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
        container.appendChild(questionDiv);
    });

    checkPersonalityCompletion(); // ëª¨ë“  ì§ˆë¬¸???µë??ˆëŠ”ì§€ ?•ì¸?˜ì—¬ ?¤ìŒ ë²„íŠ¼ ?œì„±??ë¹„í™œ?±í™”
}
function selectChoice(stage, questionId, choiceLetter, element) {
    // ê°™ì? ì§ˆë¬¸???¤ë¥¸ ? íƒì§€??? íƒ ?´ì œ
    const questionCard = element.closest('.question-card');
    questionCard.querySelectorAll('.choice-item').forEach(item => {
        item.classList.remove('selected');
    });
    
    // ?„ì¬ ? íƒì§€ ? íƒ
    element.classList.add('selected');
    element.querySelector('input[type="radio"]').checked = true;
    
    if (stage === 'situation') {
        checkSituationCompletion();
    } else if (stage === 'personality') {
        checkPersonalityCompletion();
    }
}

// testlogic.js - checkSituationCompletion ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??„ë˜?€ ê°™ì´ ?˜ì •?©ë‹ˆ??
function checkSituationCompletion() {
    // ?”ë©´???¤ì œë¡??Œë”ë§ëœ ì§ˆë¬¸ ì¹´ë“œ(.question-card)???˜ë? ê¸°ì??¼ë¡œ ì´?ì§ˆë¬¸ ?˜ë? ?Œì•…?©ë‹ˆ??
    const totalQuestions = document.querySelectorAll('#situationQuestionsContainer .question-card').length;
    const answeredQuestions = document.querySelectorAll('#situationQuestionsContainer input[type="radio"]:checked').length;
    const btn = document.getElementById('stage2SituationBtn');

    if (btn) { // ë²„íŠ¼??ì¡´ì¬?˜ëŠ”ì§€ ë¨¼ì? ?•ì¸?©ë‹ˆ?? (?¤ë¥˜ ë°©ì?)
      btn.disabled = answeredQuestions < totalQuestions;
    }
}

// testlogic.js - checkPersonalityCompletion ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??„ë˜?€ ê°™ì´ ?˜ì •?©ë‹ˆ??

function checkPersonalityCompletion() {
    // ?”ë©´???¤ì œë¡??Œë”ë§ëœ ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸ ì¹´ë“œ(.question-card)???˜ë? ê¸°ì??¼ë¡œ ì´?ì§ˆë¬¸ ?˜ë? ?Œì•…?©ë‹ˆ??
    // ê°œì¸?”ëœ ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸?€ ??ƒ 4ê°œê? ?œì‹œ?©ë‹ˆ??
    const totalQuestions = document.querySelectorAll('#personalityQuestionsContainer .question-card').length;
    const answeredQuestions = document.querySelectorAll('#personalityQuestionsContainer input[type="radio"]:checked').length;
    const btn = document.getElementById('stage2PersonalityBtn');

    if (btn) { // ë²„íŠ¼???¤ì œë¡?ì¡´ì¬?˜ëŠ”ì§€ ?•ì¸?©ë‹ˆ??(?¤ë¥˜ ë°©ì?).
        // ëª¨ë“  ì§ˆë¬¸???µë??ˆì„ ?Œë§Œ ë²„íŠ¼???œì„±?”í•©?ˆë‹¤.
        btn.disabled = answeredQuestions < totalQuestions;
    }
}



// testlogic.js - renderResponseSummary ?¨ìˆ˜ ?„ì²´ë¥??„ë˜ ?´ìš©?¼ë¡œ ?€ì²´í•©?ˆë‹¤.



// 2?¨ê³„ ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸ -> 3?¨ê³„ ?¨ë³´?©ìœ¼ë¡?ë°”ë¡œ ?´ë™?˜ëŠ” ???¨ìˆ˜
function proceedToStage3Onboarding() {
    // (ê¸°ì¡´ showResponseSummary ?¨ìˆ˜?ì„œ ê°€?¸ì˜¨) ?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?‘ë‹µ ?˜ì§‘ ë¡œì§
    const personalityResponses = [];
    const personalizedPersonalityQuestions = testSystem.currentPersonalityQuestions || [];

    personalizedPersonalityQuestions.forEach(questionData => {
        const questionId = questionData.id;
        const selectedRadio = document.querySelector(`input[name="question_${questionId}"]:checked`);

        if (selectedRadio) {
            const choiceLetter = selectedRadio.value;
            const choiceText = selectedRadio.dataset.choiceText;
            const choiceCategory = selectedRadio.dataset.choiceCategory;

            personalityResponses.push({
                questionId: questionId,
                questionText: questionData.text,
                selectedChoice: {
                    letter: choiceLetter,
                    text: choiceText,
                    category: choiceCategory
                }
            });
        }
    });

    testSystem.stage2_personality_responses = personalityResponses;
    console.log("?±í–¥ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?‘ë‹µ ?˜ì§‘ ?„ë£Œ: ", testSystem.stage2_personality_responses);
    
    

    // ?”ë©´ ?„í™˜
    document.getElementById('stage2Personality').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('stage3_onboarding').style.display = 'block';
    console.log('??3?¨ê³„ ?¨ë³´???”ë©´?¼ë¡œ ?´ë™?©ë‹ˆ??');
}

function renderStage3Page(pageNumber) { // pageNumber??1 ?ëŠ” 2
    // ?ŒŸ ì¤‘ìš”: completeStage3Questions?€ stage3SelectedQuestionIds ë³€?˜ê?
    // ???¨ìˆ˜?ì„œ ?‘ê·¼ ê°€?¥í•œ ë²”ìœ„???ˆì–´???©ë‹ˆ?? (ë³´í†µ ?„ì—­ ë³€???ëŠ” testSystem???ì„±)

    if (!completeStage3Questions || !stage3SelectedQuestionIds) {
        console.error("? ï¸ 3?¨ê³„ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´???ëŠ” ? íƒ??ì§ˆë¬¸ IDê°€ ì¤€ë¹„ë˜ì§€ ?Šì•„ ?˜ì´ì§€ë¥??Œë”ë§í•  ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.");
        // ?¬ìš©?ì—ê²??¤ë¥˜ ë©”ì‹œì§€ë¥?ë³´ì—¬ì£¼ê±°?? ?´ì „ ?˜ì´ì§€ë¡??Œë ¤ë³´ë‚´???±ì˜ ì²˜ë¦¬ê°€ ?„ìš”?????ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.
        const containerId = pageNumber === 1 ? 'reflectionContainer1' : 'reflectionContainer2';
        const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
        if(container) container.innerHTML = "<p>ì§ˆë¬¸??ë¶ˆëŸ¬?¤ëŠ” ??ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë°œìƒ?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. ?´ì „ ?¨ê³„ë¡??Œì•„ê°€ ?¤ì‹œ ?œë„?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.</p>";
        return;
    }

    let questionIdToRender;
    let containerId;

    if (pageNumber === 1) {
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.firstQuestionId;
        containerId = 'reflectionContainer1';
    } else if (pageNumber === 2) {
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.secondQuestionId;
        containerId = 'reflectionContainer2';
    } else {
        console.error("?˜ëª»???˜ì´ì§€ ë²ˆí˜¸?…ë‹ˆ??", pageNumber);
        return;
    }

    if (!questionIdToRender) {
        console.error(`? ï¸ ${pageNumber}?˜ì´ì§€???´ë‹¹?˜ëŠ” ì§ˆë¬¸ IDë¥?ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.`);
        const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
        if(container) container.innerHTML = `<p>${pageNumber}?˜ì´ì§€ ì§ˆë¬¸??ë¶ˆëŸ¬?¤ëŠ” ???¤íŒ¨?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. ê´€ë¦¬ì?ê²Œ ë¬¸ì˜?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!container) {
        console.error(`ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆ ID ${containerId}ë¥?ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.`);
        return;
    }
    
    // 'completeStage3Questions' ë°°ì—´?ì„œ ?´ë‹¹ ID??ì§ˆë¬¸ ê°ì²´ë¥?ì°¾ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.
    const questionToDisplay = completeStage3Questions.find(q => q.id === questionIdToRender);

    if (!questionToDisplay) {
        console.error(`ID ${questionIdToRender}???´ë‹¹?˜ëŠ” ì§ˆë¬¸??completeStage3Questions?ì„œ ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.`);
        container.innerHTML = `<p>ID ${questionIdToRender} ì§ˆë¬¸???œì‹œ?˜ëŠ” ??ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë°œìƒ?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    console.log(`?“ ${pageNumber}?˜ì´ì§€ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?Œë”ë§?(ID: ${questionIdToRender}):`, questionToDisplay.title);
    
    // --- â¬‡ï¸ ???„ë˜??ê¸°ì¡´ renderStage3Page ?¨ìˆ˜?ì„œ ì§ˆë¬¸ ê°ì²´ë¥?ë°›ì•„ ?”ë©´??ê·¸ë¦¬??ë¡œì§ê³?? ì‚¬??ê²ƒì…?ˆë‹¤. ---
    //    questionToDisplay ê°ì²´ (id, title, questions, examples, reflectionCategory, attractionCategories ?¬í•¨)ë¥?    //    ?¬ìš©?˜ì—¬ HTML??êµ¬ì„±?©ë‹ˆ??
    container.innerHTML = ''; // ê¸°ì¡´ ?´ìš© ì´ˆê¸°??
    const questionCard = document.createElement('div');
    questionCard.className = 'reflection-question-card';
    // questionToDisplay ê°ì²´???ì„±?¤ì„ ?¬ìš©?˜ì—¬ HTML ?´ìš©??ì±„ì›?ˆë‹¤.
    // ?ˆì‹œë¡?titleê³?pageNumberë§??¬ìš©?ˆì?ë§? ê¸°ì¡´ ?Œë”ë§?ë¡œì§???¬ê¸°???ìš©?˜ì„¸??
    questionCard.innerHTML = `
        <div class="reflection-question-header">
    <div class="reflection-question-title">${questionToDisplay.title}</div>
    <div class="reflection-question-number">${pageNumber}/3</div>
</div>
        
        <div class="attraction-guide">
            <div class="attraction-guide-icon">??/div>
            <div class="attraction-guide-text">
                <strong>ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ?œë? ?œìš©?˜ì„¸??</strong><br>
                ?µë? ?‘ì„± ??ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ?œë? ? íƒ?˜ë©´ ???ë????œí˜„???????ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="reflection-sub-questions">
            ${questionToDisplay.questions.map((subQuestion, index) => `
                <div class="reflection-sub-question">
                    <div class="reflection-sub-question-title">
                        ${pageNumber}-${index + 1}. ${subQuestion} 
                        ${ typeof subQuestion.replace === 'function' ? subQuestion.replace(/^\d+-\d+\.\s*/, '') : subQuestion } 
                        </div>
                    
                    <div class="helper-buttons">
                       
                        <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showExample(${questionToDisplay.id}, ${index})">?’¡ ?ˆì‹œ ë³´ê¸°</button>
                        <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showTemplate(${questionToDisplay.id}, ${index})">?“ ?œí”Œë¦?/button>
                        <button class="helper-btn attraction-keyword-btn" onclick="showAttractionKeywords(${questionToDisplay.id}, ${index})">
                            ??<strong>ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ??? íƒ</strong> ??                        </button>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="textarea-container">
                        <div class="selected-keywords" id="selectedKeywords_${questionToDisplay.id}_${index}">
                            <div class="keywords-label">? íƒ??ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ??</div>
                            <div class="keywords-tags">
                                <div class="no-keywords">?„ì§ ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œê? ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        
                        <textarea 
                            class="reflection-textarea" 
                            placeholder="?ìœ ë¡?²Œ ?ê°???ì–´ì£¼ì„¸??.."
                            id="reflection_${questionToDisplay.id}_${index}"
                            onfocus="window.currentTextarea = this; window.currentQuestionId = ${questionToDisplay.id}; window.currentSubIndex = ${index};"
                            oninput="saveReflectionAnswer(${questionToDisplay.id}, ${index}, this.value)"
                        ></textarea>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('')}
        </div>
    `;
    container.appendChild(questionCard);
    // --- â¬†ï¸ ?¬ê¸°ê¹Œì? ê¸°ì¡´ ?Œë”ë§?ë¡œì§ê³?? ì‚¬?˜ê²Œ HTML êµ¬ì„± â¬†ï¸ ---
    
    // ?´ì „ ?µë? ë³µì› ë¡œì§???ˆë‹¤ë©? questionToDisplay.idë¥??¬ìš©?˜ì—¬ ?¸ì¶œ?©ë‹ˆ??
    restoreReflectionAnswers(questionToDisplay.id);
}

function goToSelectPage() {
    console.log("ë§¤ë ¥ ? íƒ ?˜ì´ì§€ë¡??´ë™ ?œì‘");
    
    try {
        // ?„ì¬ê¹Œì????°ì´???€??        if (typeof completeStage3Timer === 'function') {
            completeStage3Timer();
        }
        if (typeof collectStage3Responses === 'function') {
            collectStage3Responses(); 
        }
        if (typeof autoSaveProgress === 'function') {
            autoSaveProgress();
        }
        
        // ???˜ê²½?ì„œ??select.htmlë¡?ì§ì ‘ ?´ë™
        if (window.ReactNativeWebView) {
            // ???˜ê²½????            window.ReactNativeWebView.postMessage(JSON.stringify({ type: 'navigation', screen: 'next' }));
        } else {
            // ???˜ê²½????            console.log("???˜ê²½?ì„œ select.htmlë¡??´ë™");
            window.location.href = 'select.html';
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("goToSelectPage ?¤ë¥˜:", error);
        // ?¤ë¥˜ ë°œìƒ?œì—??ê°•ì œë¡??´ë™
        window.location.href = 'select.html';
    }
}

// ?¨ìˆ˜ ?´ë¦„????ëª…í™•?˜ê²Œ ë°”ê¿‰?ˆë‹¤.
function goToNextJourney() { 
    console.log("1-3?¨ê³„ ë§¤ë ¥ ?ìƒ‰ ?„ë£Œ! ?¤ìŒ ?¬ì •?¼ë¡œ ?´ë™?©ë‹ˆ??");
    
    // 3?¨ê³„ê¹Œì???ëª¨ë“  ?°ì´?°ë? ?˜ì§‘?˜ê³  ?€?¥í•˜??ê²ƒì? ê·¸ë?ë¡?? ì??©ë‹ˆ??
    completeStage3Timer();
    collectStage3Responses(); 
    autoSaveProgress();

    // [?µì‹¬!] ?¤ìŒ ?”ë©´(select.html)?¼ë¡œ ?´ë™?˜ë¼??? í˜¸ë¥??±ìœ¼ë¡?ë³´ëƒ…?ˆë‹¤.
    if (window.ReactNativeWebView) {
        window.ReactNativeWebView.postMessage(JSON.stringify({ type: 'navigation', screen: 'next' }));
    } else {
        // ??ë¸Œë¼?°ì??ì„œ ?ŒìŠ¤?¸í•  ?Œë? ?„í•œ ê²½ê³ ì°?        alert("?ŒìŠ¤???„ë£Œ! ?¤ìŒ ?¨ê³„ë¡??´ë™?©ë‹ˆ?? (???˜ê²½???„ë‹˜)");
    }
}

// testlogic.js ?Œì¼?ì„œ ê¸°ì¡´ collectStage3Responses ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥?ì°¾ì•„ ??ì½”ë“œë¡??„ì „??êµì²´?©ë‹ˆ??

// ??testlogic.js ?Œì¼???ˆëŠ” ëª¨ë“  collectStage3Responses ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??? œ?˜ê³ , ??ì½”ë“œë¡?êµì²´?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.

function collectStage3Responses() {
    const responses = {}; 
    const questions = completeStage3Questions || [];

    if (!stage3SelectedQuestionIds) {
        console.error("? ï¸ [collectStage3Responses] ? íƒ??3?¨ê³„ ì§ˆë¬¸ IDê°€ ?†ì–´ ?µë????˜ì§‘?????†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.");
        testSystem.stage3_responses = responses;
        return;
    }

    // 3ê°œì˜ ì§ˆë¬¸ IDë¥?ëª¨ë‘ ?˜ì§‘ ?€?ìœ¼ë¡?ì§€?•í•©?ˆë‹¤.
    const questionIdsToCollect = [
        stage3SelectedQuestionIds.firstQuestionId,
        stage3SelectedQuestionIds.secondQuestionId,
        stage3SelectedQuestionIds.thirdQuestionId
    ];

    questionIdsToCollect.forEach(questionId => {
        if (!questionId) return;

        const questionGroup = questions.find(q => q.id === questionId);
        if (questionGroup) {
            const subResponses = {};
            const keywords = {};

            questionGroup.questions.forEach((subQuestionText, subIndex) => {
                // ?—â—??[?µì‹¬!] div?ì„œ ?µë???ê°€?¸ì˜¤ê¸??„í•´ .innerHTML???¬ìš©?©ë‹ˆ??
                const answerBox = document.getElementById(`reflection_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
                subResponses[subIndex] = answerBox ? answerBox.innerHTML.trim() : "[?µë? ?†ìŒ]";

                // ?¤ì›Œ?œë„ ?¨ê»˜ ?˜ì§‘?©ë‹ˆ??
                const keywordsContainer = document.getElementById(`selectedKeywords_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
                if (keywordsContainer) {
                    const keywordTags = keywordsContainer.querySelectorAll('.keyword-tag');
                    keywords[subIndex] = Array.from(keywordTags).map(tag => tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim());
                }
            });

            responses[questionId] = {
                id: questionGroup.id,
                groupTitle: questionGroup.title,
                responses: subResponses,
                keywords: keywords
            };
        }
    });
    
    testSystem.stage3_responses = responses;
    console.log("?“ 3?¨ê³„ ?‘ë‹µ 3ê°?ëª¨ë‘ ?˜ì§‘ ?„ë£Œ:", testSystem.stage3_responses);
}

// ==================== ?„ìš°ë¯?ê¸°ëŠ¥??====================

// ê¸°ì¡´ ì½”ë“œ??ê·¸ë?ë¡??ê³ , ?„ë˜ ?¨ìˆ˜?¤ì„ ì¶”ê??˜ì„¸??







function insertKeyword(keyword) {
    if (window.currentTextarea) {
        const current = window.currentTextarea.value;
        window.currentTextarea.value = current + (current ? ' ' : '') + keyword;
        window.currentTextarea.focus();
    }
}

function closeModal(modalId) {
    document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
}

// ?„ì—­ ë³€??ì¶”ê? (?Œì¼ ìµœìƒ??ê·¼ì²˜??
window.currentTextarea = null;

// ê¸°ì¡´ renderReflectionQuestions ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??˜ì •?˜ì—¬ ë²„íŠ¼?¤ì´ ?‘ë™?˜ë„ë¡??…ë°?´íŠ¸
function renderReflectionQuestions(questionSet, containerId) {
    const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    
    const html = `
        <div class="reflection-question-card">
            <div class="reflection-question-header">
                <div class="reflection-question-title">${questionSet.title}</div>
                <div class="reflection-question-number">${questionSet.id}/4</div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="reflection-sub-questions">
                ${questionSet.questions.map((question, index) => `
                    <div class="reflection-sub-question">
                        <div class="reflection-sub-question-title">${question}</div>
                        <div class="helper-buttons">
                            <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showExamples(getReflectionQuestions()[${questionSet.id - 1}], ${index})">
                                ?’¡ ?µë? ?ˆì‹œ ë³´ê¸°
                            </button>
                            <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showTemplate(getReflectionQuestions()[${questionSet.id - 1}], ${index})">
                                ?“ ê¸€?°ê¸° ?œí”Œë¦?                            </button>
                            <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showAttractionKeywords()">
                                ??ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ??? íƒ
                            </button>
                            <button class="helper-btn skip">??¸ ê±´ë„ˆ?°ê¸°</button>
                            <button class="helper-btn bookmark">?”– ?˜ì¤‘???‘ì„±</button>
                        </div>
                        <textarea 
                            class="reflection-textarea" 
                            placeholder="?´ê³³???ìœ ë¡?²Œ ?µë????‘ì„±?´ì£¼?¸ìš”..." 
                            data-question-id="${questionSet.id}-${index + 1}"
                            onfocus="window.currentTextarea = this"
                        ></textarea>
                    </div>
                `).join('')}
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    container.innerHTML = html;
}// ê¸°ì¡´ ì½”ë“œ??ê·¸ë?ë¡??ê³ , ?„ë˜ ?¨ìˆ˜?¤ì„ ì¶”ê??˜ì„¸??

// ?¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ì¶”ê? ?¨ìˆ˜
function addKeywordTag(keyword) {
    const questionId = window.currentQuestionId;
    const subIndex = window.currentSubIndex;
    
    if (!questionId || subIndex === undefined) return;
    
    const keywordsContainer = document.getElementById(`selectedKeywords_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    const tagsContainer = keywordsContainer.querySelector('.keywords-tags');
    
    // ?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì¸ì§€ ?•ì¸
    const existingTags = tagsContainer.querySelectorAll('.keyword-tag');
    const existingKeywords = Array.from(existingTags).map(tag => tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim());
    
    if (existingKeywords.includes(keyword)) {
        // ?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œë¼ë©?ê°•ì¡° ?¨ê³¼
        const existingTag = Array.from(existingTags).find(tag => tag.textContent.includes(keyword));
        existingTag.style.animation = 'none';
        setTimeout(() => {
            existingTag.style.animation = 'pulse 0.5s ease-in-out';
        }, 10);
        return;
    }
    
    // ?ˆë¡œ???¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ?ì„±
    const keywordTag = document.createElement('div');
    keywordTag.className = 'keyword-tag';
    keywordTag.innerHTML = `
        ${keyword}
        <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeKeywordTag(this)" title="?¤ì›Œ???œê±°">Ã—</button>
    `;
    
    tagsContainer.appendChild(keywordTag);
    
    // "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œê±°
    const noKeywordsMsg = tagsContainer.querySelector('.no-keywords');
    if (noKeywordsMsg) {
        noKeywordsMsg.remove();
    }
    
    // ëª¨ë‹¬ ?«ê¸° (? íƒ??
    // closeModal('attractionModal');
    
    console.log(`?¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ì¶”ê???);
}

// ?¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ?œê±° ?¨ìˆ˜
function removeKeywordTag(button) {
    const tag = button.parentElement;
    const keyword = tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim();
    
    tag.style.animation = 'fadeOutScale 0.3s ease-out';
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        tag.remove();
        
        // ?¤ì›Œ?œê? ëª¨ë‘ ?œê±°?˜ë©´ "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œì‹œ
        const tagsContainer = tag.parentElement;
        if (tagsContainer && tagsContainer.children.length === 0) {
            const noKeywordsMsg = document.createElement('div');
            noKeywordsMsg.className = 'no-keywords';
            noKeywordsMsg.textContent = '?„ì§ ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œê? ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤';
            tagsContainer.appendChild(noKeywordsMsg);
        }
    }, 300);
    
    console.log(`?¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ?œê±°??);
}

// ?„ì—­ ë³€??ì´ˆê¸°??(ê¸°ì¡´ window.currentTextarea = null; ?¤ìŒ??ì¶”ê?)
window.currentQuestionId = null;
window.currentSubIndex = null;

function insertKeyword(keyword) {
    if (window.currentTextarea) {
        const current = window.currentTextarea.value;
        window.currentTextarea.value = current + (current ? ' ' : '') + keyword;
        window.currentTextarea.focus();
    }
}

function closeModal(modalId) {
    document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
}

// ê¸°ì¡´ renderReflectionQuestions ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??˜ì •?˜ì—¬ ë²„íŠ¼?¤ì´ ?‘ë™?˜ë„ë¡??…ë°?´íŠ¸
function renderReflectionQuestions(questionSet, containerId) {
    const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    
    const html = `
        <div class="reflection-question-card">
            <div class="reflection-question-header">
                <div class="reflection-question-title">${questionSet.title}</div>
                <div class="reflection-question-number">${questionSet.id}/4</div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="reflection-sub-questions">
                ${questionSet.questions.map((question, index) => `
                    <div class="reflection-sub-question">
                        <div class="reflection-sub-question-title">${question}</div>
                        <div class="helper-buttons">
                            <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showExamples(getReflectionQuestions()[${questionSet.id - 1}], ${index})">
                                ?’¡ ?µë? ?ˆì‹œ ë³´ê¸°
                            </button>
                            <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showTemplate(getReflectionQuestions()[${questionSet.id - 1}], ${index})">
                                ?“ ê¸€?°ê¸° ?œí”Œë¦?                            </button>
                            <button class="helper-btn" onclick="showAttractionKeywords()">
                                ??ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ??? íƒ
                            </button>
                        
                        </div>
                        <textarea 
                            class="reflection-textarea" 
                            placeholder="?´ê³³???ìœ ë¡?²Œ ?µë????‘ì„±?´ì£¼?¸ìš”..." 
                            data-question-id="${questionSet.id}-${index + 1}"
                            onfocus="window.currentTextarea = this"
                        ></textarea>
                    </div>
                `).join('')}
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    container.innerHTML = html;
}


function insertKeyword(keyword) {
    // ?„ì¬ ?¬ì»¤?¤ëœ textarea???¤ì›Œ??ì¶”ê?
    const focusedElement = document.activeElement;
    if (focusedElement && focusedElement.classList.contains('reflection-textarea')) {
        const currentValue = focusedElement.value;
        const newValue = currentValue + (currentValue ? ', ' : '') + keyword;
        focusedElement.value = newValue;
    }
}


// testlogic.js ?Œì¼????ì½”ë“œë¡??„ì²´ë¥?êµì²´?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.

function setupSurveyValidation() {
    const form = document.getElementById('surveyForm');
    const submitBtn = document.getElementById('surveySubmitBtn');

    if (!form || !submitBtn) {
        console.error("?¤ë¬¸ì¡°ì‚¬ form ?ëŠ” ?œì¶œ ë²„íŠ¼??ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.");
        return;
    }

    // ??'skip_option_rating'???œê±°?? ?¬ë°”ë¥??„ìˆ˜ ?„ë“œ ëª©ë¡?…ë‹ˆ??
    const requiredFields = [
        'overall_satisfaction', 'discovery_help', 'recommendation',
        'stage1_rating', 'stage2_rating', 'stage3_rating',
        'needs_improvement', 'onboarding_rating', 'example_rating',
        'template_rating', 'keywords_rating', 'understanding_improvement',
        'positivity_improvement'
    ];

    function checkFormCompletion() {
        // ???¼ë””??ë²„íŠ¼ê³??¤ë¥¸ ?…ë ¥ ?„ë“œë¥?ëª…í™•??êµ¬ë¶„?˜ì—¬ ê²€ì¦í•˜???ˆë¡œ??ë¡œì§?…ë‹ˆ??
        const allCompleted = requiredFields.every(fieldName => {
            const element = form.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]`);
            if (!element) {
                // ?´ë‹¹ ?´ë¦„???”ì†Œê°€ ?„ì˜ˆ ?†ìœ¼ë©?false ë°˜í™˜
                return false; 
            }

            if (element.type === 'radio') {
                // ?€?…ì´ ?¼ë””??ë²„íŠ¼??ê²½ìš°, :checked ??ê²ƒì´ ?ˆëŠ”ì§€ ?•ì¸
                return form.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]:checked`) !== null;
            } else {
                // ?¼ë””??ë²„íŠ¼???„ë‹ ê²½ìš°(select, textarea ??, ê°’ì´ ?ˆëŠ”ì§€ ?•ì¸
                return !!element.value;
            }
        });

        // ëª¨ë“  ?„ìˆ˜ ??ª©???„ë£Œ?˜ì—ˆ???Œë§Œ ë²„íŠ¼ ?œì„±??        submitBtn.disabled = !allCompleted;
    }

    // form???´ë²¤??ë¦¬ìŠ¤?ˆë? ì¶”ê??˜ì—¬, ë³€ê²½ì´ ?ˆì„ ?Œë§ˆ??ê²€ì¦??¨ìˆ˜ë¥??¤í–‰
    form.addEventListener('change', checkFormCompletion);
    form.addEventListener('input', checkFormCompletion);

    // ?˜ì´ì§€ ë¡œë“œ ??ì´ˆê¸° ?íƒœë¥???ë²?ê²€??    checkFormCompletion();
}

// ==================== ?¤ë¬¸ì¡°ì‚¬ ?Œë”ë§?====================


// ?¤ë¬¸ ? íš¨??ê²€???¨ìˆ˜
function setupSurveyValidation() {
    const form = document.getElementById('surveyForm');
    const submitBtn = document.getElementById('surveySubmitBtn');
    
    // ?„ìˆ˜ ?„ë“œ??    const requiredFields = [
        'overall_satisfaction',
        'discovery_help', 
        'recommendation',
        'stage1_rating',
        'stage2_rating', 
        'stage3_rating',
        'needs_improvement',
        'onboarding_rating',
        'example_rating',
        'template_rating',
        'keywords_rating',
        'understanding_improvement',
        'positivity_improvement'
    ];
    
    function checkFormCompletion() {
        const allCompleted = requiredFields.every(fieldName => {
            return form.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]:checked`) || 
                   form.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]`).value;
        });
        
        submitBtn.disabled = !allCompleted;
    }
    
    // ëª¨ë“  inputê³?select???´ë²¤??ë¦¬ìŠ¤??ì¶”ê?
    form.addEventListener('change', checkFormCompletion);
    form.addEventListener('input', checkFormCompletion);
    
    // ì´ˆê¸° ?íƒœ ì²´í¬
    checkFormCompletion();
}



// ìµœì¢… ?„ë£Œ ?˜ì´ì§€ ?Œë”ë§?
// ==================== ëª¨ë‹¬ ?¸ë? ?´ë¦­???«ê¸° ====================
window.onclick = function(event) {
    const modals = ['exampleModal', 'templateModal', 'attractionModal'];
    modals.forEach(modalId => {
        const modal = document.getElementById(modalId);
        if (event.target === modal) {
            modal.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
}

// ê°œì¸?”ëœ ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ ?Œê³ ë¦¬ì¦˜
function selectPersonalizedQuestion() {
    const stage1Categories = testSystem.stage1_selections;
    const stage2Situation = testSystem.stage2_situation_responses;
    const stage2Personality = testSystem.stage2_personality_responses;
    
    // 1?¨ê³„ ë§¤ë ¥ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ë¶„ì„
    const introspectiveCategories = ['?•ì„œ???ˆì • ë°??ê¸° ?¸ì‹', '?„ë•??ë°??‘ì‹¬'];
    const socialCategories = ['? ë¨¸ê°ê° ë°??¬êµ??, '?´í•´??ë°?ê³µê° ?¥ë ¥'];
    const growthCategories = ['ì§€???¸ê¸°??ë°?ê°œë°©??, 'ëª©í‘œ ì§€?¥ì„± ë°??¼ë§'];
    
    let introspectiveScore = 0;
    let socialScore = 0;
    let growthScore = 0;
    
    // ? íƒ??ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ?ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
    stage1Categories.forEach(category => {
        if (introspectiveCategories.includes(category)) introspectiveScore += 2;
        if (socialCategories.includes(category)) socialScore += 2;
        if (growthCategories.includes(category)) growthScore += 2;
    });
    
    // 2?¨ê³„ ?‘ë‹µ ?¨í„´ ë¶„ì„
    stage2Situation.forEach(response => {
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'A') socialScore += 1;
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'C') growthScore += 1;
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'D') introspectiveScore += 1;
    });
    
    stage2Personality.forEach(response => {
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'A') {
            if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) socialScore += 1;
            if (response.questionText.includes('ê´€ê³?)) socialScore += 1;
        }
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'B') {
            if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) introspectiveScore += 1;
            if (response.questionText.includes('?€ì§ì´??)) growthScore += 1;
        }
    });
    
    // ìµœê³  ?ìˆ˜ ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ
    if (growthScore >= introspectiveScore && growthScore >= socialScore) {
        return 3; // ?±ì¥ ë°©í–¥
    } else if (socialScore >= introspectiveScore) {
        return 4; // ê´€ê³„ì„± ?´í•´
    } else {
        return 2; // ê°€ì¹˜ê? ?ìƒ‰
    }
}

function addKeywordTag(keyword) {
    const questionId = window.currentQuestionId;
    const subIndex = window.currentSubIndex;
    
    if (!questionId || subIndex === undefined) {
        console.log('?„ì¬ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?•ë³´ê°€ ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤');
        return;
    }
    
    const keywordsContainer = document.getElementById(`selectedKeywords_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    if (!keywordsContainer) {
        console.log('?¤ì›Œ??ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆë¥?ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤');
        return;
    }
    
    const tagsContainer = keywordsContainer.querySelector('.keywords-tags');
    if (!tagsContainer) {
        console.log('?œê·¸ ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆë¥?ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤');
        return;
    }
    
    // ?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì¸ì§€ ?•ì¸
    const existingTags = tagsContainer.querySelectorAll('.keyword-tag');

    if (existingKeywords.includes(keyword)) {
        alert('?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì…?ˆë‹¤!');
        return;
    }
    
    // ?ˆë¡œ???¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ?ì„±
    const keywordTag = document.createElement('div');
    keywordTag.className = 'keyword-tag';
    keywordTag.innerHTML = `
        ${keyword}
        <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeKeywordTag(this)" title="?¤ì›Œ???œê±°">Ã—</button>
    `;
    
    tagsContainer.appendChild(keywordTag);
    
    // "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œê±°
    const noKeywordsMsg = tagsContainer.querySelector('.no-keywords');
    if (noKeywordsMsg) {
        noKeywordsMsg.remove();

    console.log(`?¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ì¶”ê???);
    
    // ëª¨ë‹¬ ?«ê¸°
    closeModal('attractionModal');
}

// ?Œì¼ ë§??„ë˜??ì¶”ê?:
function selectPersonalizedQuestion() {
    const stage1Categories = testSystem.stage1_selections;
    const stage2Situation = testSystem.stage2_situation_responses;
    const stage2Personality = testSystem.stage2_personality_responses;
    
    // 1?¨ê³„ ë§¤ë ¥ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ë¶„ì„
    const introspectiveCategories = ['?•ì„œ???ˆì • ë°??ê¸° ?¸ì‹', '?„ë•??ë°??‘ì‹¬'];
    const socialCategories = ['? ë¨¸ê°ê° ë°??¬êµ??, '?´í•´??ë°?ê³µê° ?¥ë ¥'];
    const growthCategories = ['ì§€???¸ê¸°??ë°?ê°œë°©??, 'ëª©í‘œ ì§€?¥ì„± ë°??¼ë§'];
    
    let introspectiveScore = 0;
    let socialScore = 0;
    let growthScore = 0;
    
    // ? íƒ??ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ?ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
    stage1Categories.forEach(category => {
        if (introspectiveCategories.includes(category)) introspectiveScore += 2;
        if (socialCategories.includes(category)) socialScore += 2;
        if (growthCategories.includes(category)) growthScore += 2;
    });
    
    // 2?¨ê³„ ?‘ë‹µ ?¨í„´ ë¶„ì„
    stage2Situation.forEach(response => {
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'A') socialScore += 1;
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'C') growthScore += 1;
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'D') introspectiveScore += 1;
    });
    
    stage2Personality.forEach(response => {
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'A') {
            if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) socialScore += 1;
            if (response.questionText.includes('ê´€ê³?)) socialScore += 1;
        }
        if (response.selectedChoice.letter === 'B') {
            if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) introspectiveScore += 1;
            if (response.questionText.includes('?€ì§ì´??)) growthScore += 1;
        }
    });
    
    // ìµœê³  ?ìˆ˜ ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ
    if (growthScore >= introspectiveScore && growthScore >= socialScore) {
        return 3; // ?±ì¥ ë°©í–¥
    } else if (socialScore >= introspectiveScore) {
        return 4; // ê´€ê³„ì„± ?´í•´
    } else {
        return 2; // ê°€ì¹˜ê? ?ìƒ‰
    }
}

// ê¸°ì¡´ ì½”ë“œ ë§ˆì?ë§?ë¶€ë¶„ì— ?´ì–´??ì¶”ê?:

// ==================== 29ê°??ˆë¡œ???±ì°° ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´??====================

// ==================== AI ê°œì¸??ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ ?Œê³ ë¦¬ì¦˜ ====================
function selectPersonalizedQuestion() {
    const selectedCategories = testSystem.stage1_selections;
    const situationResponses = testSystem.stage2_situation_responses;
    const personalityResponses = testSystem.stage2_personality_responses;
    
    console.log('?¤– AI ê°œì¸??ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ ?œì‘:', {
        categories: selectedCategories,
        situation: situationResponses,
        personality: personalityResponses
    });
    

    
    // ê°??ì—­ë³??ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
    let valueScore = 0;    // ê°€ì¹˜íƒêµ?(8-14)
    let growthScore = 0;   // ?±ì¥?êµ¬ (15-22)
    let relationScore = 0; // ê´€ê³„íƒêµ?(23-29)
    
    // 1?¨ê³„ ë§¤ë ¥ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ë³??ìˆ˜ ë¶€??    selectedCategories.forEach(category => {
        switch(category) {
            case "?„ë•??ë°??‘ì‹¬":
            case "?±ì‹¤??ë°?ì±…ì„ê°?:
                valueScore += 3;
                break;
            case "?•ì„œ???ˆì • ë°??ê¸° ?¸ì‹":
                valueScore += 2;
                growthScore += 1;
                break;
            case "ì§€???¸ê¸°??ë°?ê°œë°©??:
            case "ëª©í‘œ ì§€?¥ì„± ë°??¼ë§":
                growthScore += 3;
                break;
            case "?´í•´??ë°?ê³µê° ?¥ë ¥":
            case "? ë¨¸ê°ê° ë°??¬êµ??:
                relationScore += 3;
                break;
        }
    });
    
    // 2?¨ê³„ ?‘ë‹µ ?¨í„´ ë¶„ì„
    situationResponses.forEach(response => {
        const choice = response.selectedChoice.letter;
        switch(choice) {
            case 'A': relationScore += 1; break;
            case 'B': valueScore += 1; break;
            case 'C': growthScore += 1; break;
            case 'D': valueScore += 1; break;
        }
    });
    
    personalityResponses.forEach(response => {
        const choice = response.selectedChoice.letter;
        switch(choice) {
            case 'A': 
                if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) relationScore += 1;
                else if (response.questionText.includes('ê´€ê³?)) relationScore += 1;
                else growthScore += 1;
                break;
            case 'B':
                if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) valueScore += 1;
                else valueScore += 1;
                break;
        }
    });
    
    console.log('?¯ ?ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚° ê²°ê³¼:', {
        valueScore,
        growthScore,
        relationScore
    });
    
    // ìµœê³  ?ìˆ˜ ?ì—­ ê²°ì •
    let selectedCategory;
    let questionIds;
    
    if (growthScore >= valueScore && growthScore >= relationScore) {
        selectedCategory = "?±ì¥?êµ¬";
        questionIds = [15, 16, 17, 18, 19, 20, 21, 22];
    } else if (relationScore >= valueScore) {
        selectedCategory = "ê´€ê³„íƒêµ?;
        questionIds = [23, 24, 25, 26, 27, 28, 29];
    } else {
        selectedCategory = "ê°€ì¹˜íƒêµ?;
        questionIds = [8, 9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14];
    }
    
    // ?´ë‹¹ ?ì—­?ì„œ ?œë¤ ? íƒ
    const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * questionIds.length);
    const selectedQuestionId = questionIds[randomIndex];
    
    console.log('??? íƒ???ì—­:', selectedCategory);
    console.log('??? íƒ??ì§ˆë¬¸ ID:', selectedQuestionId);
    
    return selectedQuestionId;
}

// ê²½í—˜ ?êµ¬ ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ (??ƒ 1-7 ì¤??˜ë‚˜)
function selectExperienceQuestion() {
    const experienceQuestionIds = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7];
    const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * experienceQuestionIds.length);
    return experienceQuestionIds[randomIndex];
}

// testlogic.js ?Œì¼ ??function renderStage3Page(pageNumber) {
    if (!completeStage3Questions || !stage3SelectedQuestionIds) {
        console.error("? ï¸ [renderStage3Page] 3?¨ê³„ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´???ëŠ” IDê°€ ì¤€ë¹„ë˜ì§€ ?Šì•˜?µë‹ˆ??");
        return;

    let questionIdToRender;

    if (pageNumber === 1) {
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.firstQuestionId;
    } else if (pageNumber === 2) {
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.secondQuestionId;
     } else if (pageNumber === 3) { 
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.thirdQuestionId;
        containerId = 'reflectionContainer3'; // 3ë²ˆì§¸ ?˜ì´ì§€??ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆ ID
    } else {
        console.error("[renderStage3Page] ?˜ëª»???˜ì´ì§€ ë²ˆí˜¸:", pageNumber);
        return;
    }

    if (!questionIdToRender) {
        console.error(`? ï¸ ${pageNumber}?˜ì´ì§€???´ë‹¹?˜ëŠ” ì§ˆë¬¸ IDë¥?ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.`);

    renderReflectionQuestion(questionIdToRender, containerId, pageNumber);
}

// ==================== ?µë? ?€??ë°?ë³µì› ====================
function saveReflectionAnswer(questionId, subIndex, value) {
    if (!testSystem.stage3_responses) {
        testSystem.stage3_responses = {};
    }
    
    if (!testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId]) {
        testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId] = {};
    }
    
    testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId][subIndex] = value;
    console.log('?’¾ ?µë? ?€??', questionId, subIndex, value.substring(0, 30) + '...');
}

function restoreReflectionAnswers(questionId) {
    if (testSystem.stage3_responses && testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId]) {
        Object.keys(testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId]).forEach(subIndex => {
            const answerBox = document.getElementById(`reflection_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
            if (answerBox) {
                // 'value'ë¥?'innerHTML'ë¡?ë³€ê²?                answerBox.innerHTML = testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId][subIndex];
            }
        });
    }
}

// ==================== ?„ìš°ë¯?ê¸°ëŠ¥??====================
function skipQuestion(questionId, subIndex) {
    const textarea = document.getElementById(`reflection_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    if (textarea) {
        textarea.value = "[?¨ìŠ¤??";
        textarea.style.background = "#f7fafc";
        saveReflectionAnswer(questionId, subIndex, "[?¨ìŠ¤??");
    }
}






// ==================== ?¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ê´€ë¦?====================
function addKeywordTag(keyword) {
    const questionId = window.currentQuestionId;
    const subIndex = window.currentSubIndex;
    
    if (!questionId || subIndex === undefined) return;
    
    const keywordsContainer = document.getElementById(`selectedKeywords_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    const tagsContainer = keywordsContainer.querySelector('.keywords-tags');
    
    // ?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì¸ì§€ ?•ì¸
    const existingTags = tagsContainer.querySelectorAll('.keyword-tag');
    const existingKeywords = Array.from(existingTags).map(tag => tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim());
    
    if (existingKeywords.includes(keyword)) {
        alert('?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì…?ˆë‹¤!');
        return;
    }
    
    // "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œê±°
    const noKeywordsMsg = tagsContainer.querySelector('.no-keywords');
    if (noKeywordsMsg) {
        noKeywordsMsg.remove();
    }
    
    // ?ˆë¡œ???¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ?ì„±
    const keywordTag = document.createElement('div');
    keywordTag.className = 'keyword-tag';
    keywordTag.innerHTML = `
        ${keyword}
        <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeKeywordTag(this)" title="?¤ì›Œ???œê±°">Ã—</button>
    `;
    
    tagsContainer.appendChild(keywordTag);
    console.log(`???¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ì¶”ê???);
    
    // ëª¨ë‹¬ ?«ê¸°
    closeModal('attractionModal');
}

function removeKeywordTag(button) {
    const tag = button.parentElement;
    const keyword = tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim();
    
    tag.remove();
    
    // ?¤ì›Œ?œê? ëª¨ë‘ ?œê±°?˜ë©´ "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œì‹œ
    const tagsContainer = tag.parentElement;
    if (tagsContainer && tagsContainer.children.length === 0) {
        const noKeywordsMsg = document.createElement('div');
        noKeywordsMsg.className = 'no-keywords';
        noKeywordsMsg.textContent = '?„ì§ ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œê? ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤';
        tagsContainer.appendChild(noKeywordsMsg);
    }
    
    console.log(`?—‘ï¸??¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ?œê±°??);
}

// ==================== ?¤ë¬¸ì¡°ì‚¬ ?Œë”ë§?====================


function checkSurveyCompletion() {
    const requiredFields = ['overall_satisfaction', 'recommendation'];
    let allCompleted = true;
    
    requiredFields.forEach(fieldName => {
        const field = document.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]:checked`);
        if (!field) {
            allCompleted = false;
        }
    });
    
    document.getElementById('surveySubmitBtn').disabled = !allCompleted;
}

// ==================== AI ê°œì¸??ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ ?Œê³ ë¦¬ì¦˜ ====================
function selectPersonalizedQuestion() {
    const selectedCategories = testSystem.stage1_selections;
    const situationResponses = testSystem.stage2_situation_responses;
    const personalityResponses = testSystem.stage2_personality_responses;
    
    console.log('?¤– AI ê°œì¸??ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ ?œì‘:', {
        categories: selectedCategories,
        situation: situationResponses,
        personality: personalityResponses
    });
    
    // ê°??ì—­ë³??ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
    let valueScore = 0;    // ê°€ì¹˜íƒêµ?(8-14)
    let growthScore = 0;   // ?±ì¥?êµ¬ (15-22)
    let relationScore = 0; // ê´€ê³„íƒêµ?(23-29)
    
    // 1?¨ê³„ ë§¤ë ¥ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ë³??ìˆ˜ ë¶€??    selectedCategories.forEach(category => {
        switch(category) {
            case "?„ë•??ë°??‘ì‹¬":
            case "?±ì‹¤??ë°?ì±…ì„ê°?:
                valueScore += 3;
                break;
            case "?•ì„œ???ˆì • ë°??ê¸° ?¸ì‹":
                valueScore += 2;
                growthScore += 1;
                break;
            case "ì§€???¸ê¸°??ë°?ê°œë°©??:
            case "ëª©í‘œ ì§€?¥ì„± ë°??¼ë§":
                growthScore += 3;
                break;
            case "?´í•´??ë°?ê³µê° ?¥ë ¥":
            case "? ë¨¸ê°ê° ë°??¬êµ??:
                relationScore += 3;
                break;
        }
    });
    
    // 2?¨ê³„ ?‘ë‹µ ?¨í„´ ë¶„ì„
    situationResponses.forEach(response => {
        const choice = response.selectedChoice.letter;
        switch(choice) {
            case 'A': relationScore += 1; break;
            case 'B': valueScore += 1; break;
            case 'C': growthScore += 1; break;
            case 'D': valueScore += 1; break;
        }
    });
    
    personalityResponses.forEach(response => {
        const choice = response.selectedChoice.letter;
        switch(choice) {
            case 'A': 
                if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) relationScore += 1;
                else if (response.questionText.includes('ê´€ê³?)) relationScore += 1;
                else growthScore += 1;
                break;
            case 'B':
                if (response.questionText.includes('?ë„ˆì§€')) valueScore += 1;
                else valueScore += 1;
                break;
        }
    });
    
    console.log('?¯ ?ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚° ê²°ê³¼:', {
        valueScore,
        growthScore,
        relationScore
    });
    
    // ìµœê³  ?ìˆ˜ ?ì—­ ê²°ì •
    let selectedCategory;
    let questionIds;
    
    if (growthScore >= valueScore && growthScore >= relationScore) {
        selectedCategory = "?±ì¥?êµ¬";
        questionIds = [15, 16, 17, 18, 19, 20, 21, 22];
    } else if (relationScore >= valueScore) {
        selectedCategory = "ê´€ê³„íƒêµ?;
        questionIds = [23, 24, 25, 26, 27, 28, 29];
    } else {
        selectedCategory = "ê°€ì¹˜íƒêµ?;
        questionIds = [8, 9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14];
    }
    
    // ?´ë‹¹ ?ì—­?ì„œ ?œë¤ ? íƒ
    const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * questionIds.length);
    const selectedQuestionId = questionIds[randomIndex];
    
    console.log('??? íƒ???ì—­:', selectedCategory);
    console.log('??? íƒ??ì§ˆë¬¸ ID:', selectedQuestionId);
    
    return selectedQuestionId;
}

// ê²½í—˜ ?êµ¬ ì§ˆë¬¸ ? íƒ (??ƒ 1-7 ì¤??˜ë‚˜)
function selectExperienceQuestion() {
    const experienceQuestionIds = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7];
    const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * experienceQuestionIds.length);
    return experienceQuestionIds[randomIndex];
}

// ==================== ?±ì°° ì§ˆë¬¸ ?Œë”ë§?====================
// testlogic.js ?Œì¼ ??renderStage3Page ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??„ë˜?€ ê°™ì´ ?˜ì •?©ë‹ˆ??

// ????'?„ê²°?? ì½”ë“œë¡?ê¸°ì¡´??ëª¨ë“  renderStage3Page ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??€ì²´í•´ì£¼ì„¸??

function renderStage3Page(pageNumber) {
    if (!completeStage3Questions || !stage3SelectedQuestionIds) {
        console.error("? ï¸ [renderStage3Page] 3?¨ê³„ ì§ˆë¬¸ ?°ì´???ëŠ” IDê°€ ì¤€ë¹„ë˜ì§€ ?Šì•˜?µë‹ˆ??");
        return;
    }

    let questionIdToRender;
    const containerId = `reflectionContainer${pageNumber}`; // ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆ IDë¥??™ì ?¼ë¡œ ?ì„±?©ë‹ˆ??

    if (pageNumber === 1) {
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.firstQuestionId;
    } else if (pageNumber === 2) {
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.secondQuestionId;
    } else if (pageNumber === 3) {
        // 3ë²ˆì§¸ ?˜ì´ì§€ë¥??„í•œ ë¡œì§
        questionIdToRender = stage3SelectedQuestionIds.thirdQuestionId;
    } else {
        console.error("[renderStage3Page] ?˜ëª»???˜ì´ì§€ ë²ˆí˜¸?…ë‹ˆ??", pageNumber);
        return;
    }

    // ì§ˆë¬¸ IDê°€ ?†ëŠ” ê²½ìš°(undefined)???€??ë°©ì–´ ì½”ë“œ
    if (!questionIdToRender) {
        console.error(`? ï¸ ${pageNumber}?˜ì´ì§€???´ë‹¹?˜ëŠ” ì§ˆë¬¸ IDë¥?ì°¾ì„ ???†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. (IDê°€ undefined) startStage3 ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??•ì¸?´ì£¼?¸ìš”.`);
        const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
        if (container) {
            container.innerHTML = `<p>ì§ˆë¬¸??ë¶ˆëŸ¬?¤ëŠ” ???¤íŒ¨?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤. ID ? íƒ ë¡œì§??ë¬¸ì œê°€ ?ˆìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.</p>`;
        }
        return;
    }
    
    // ?¤ì œ ì§ˆë¬¸???”ë©´??ê·¸ë¦¬???¨ìˆ˜ ?¸ì¶œ
    renderReflectionQuestion(questionIdToRender, containerId, pageNumber);
}

// testlogic.js ?Œì¼ ??renderReflectionQuestion ?¨ìˆ˜ë¥??„ë˜ ?´ìš©?¼ë¡œ ?„ì²´ êµì²´?©ë‹ˆ??



// ==================== ?µë? ?€??ë°?ë³µì› ====================
function saveReflectionAnswer(questionId, subIndex, value) {
    if (!testSystem.stage3_responses) {
        testSystem.stage3_responses = {};
    }
    
    if (!testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId]) {
        testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId] = {};
    }
    
    testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId][subIndex] = value;
    console.log('?’¾ ?µë? ?€??', questionId, subIndex, value.substring(0, 30) + '...');
}

function restoreReflectionAnswers(questionId) {
    if (testSystem.stage3_responses && testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId]) {
        Object.keys(testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId]).forEach(subIndex => {
            const textarea = document.getElementById(`reflection_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
            if (textarea) {
                textarea.value = testSystem.stage3_responses[questionId][subIndex];
            }
        });
    }
}

// ==================== ?„ìš°ë¯?ê¸°ëŠ¥??====================


// ==================== ?¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ê´€ë¦?====================
function addKeywordTag(keyword) {
    const questionId = window.currentQuestionId;
    const subIndex = window.currentSubIndex;
    
    if (!questionId || subIndex === undefined) return;
    
    const keywordsContainer = document.getElementById(`selectedKeywords_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    const tagsContainer = keywordsContainer.querySelector('.keywords-tags');
    
    // ?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì¸ì§€ ?•ì¸
    const existingTags = tagsContainer.querySelectorAll('.keyword-tag');
    const existingKeywords = Array.from(existingTags).map(tag => tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim());
    
    if (existingKeywords.includes(keyword)) {
        alert('?´ë? ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œì…?ˆë‹¤!');
        return;
    }
    
    // "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œê±°
    const noKeywordsMsg = tagsContainer.querySelector('.no-keywords');
    if (noKeywordsMsg) {
        noKeywordsMsg.remove();
    }
    
    // ?ˆë¡œ???¤ì›Œ???œê·¸ ?ì„±
    const keywordTag = document.createElement('div');
    keywordTag.className = 'keyword-tag';
    keywordTag.innerHTML = `
        ${keyword}
        <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeKeywordTag(this)" title="?¤ì›Œ???œê±°">Ã—</button>
    `;
    
    tagsContainer.appendChild(keywordTag);
    console.log(`???¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ì¶”ê???);
    
    // ëª¨ë‹¬ ?«ê¸°
    closeModal('attractionModal');
}

function removeKeywordTag(button) {
    const tag = button.parentElement;
    const keyword = tag.textContent.replace('Ã—', '').trim();
    
    tag.remove();
    
    // ?¤ì›Œ?œê? ëª¨ë‘ ?œê±°?˜ë©´ "?¤ì›Œ???†ìŒ" ë©”ì‹œì§€ ?œì‹œ
    const tagsContainer = tag.parentElement;
    if (tagsContainer && tagsContainer.children.length === 0) {
        const noKeywordsMsg = document.createElement('div');
        noKeywordsMsg.className = 'no-keywords';
        noKeywordsMsg.textContent = '?„ì§ ? íƒ???¤ì›Œ?œê? ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤';
        tagsContainer.appendChild(noKeywordsMsg);
    }
    
    console.log(`?—‘ï¸??¤ì›Œ??"${keyword}" ?œê±°??);
}

// ==================== ?¤ë¬¸ì¡°ì‚¬ ?Œë”ë§?====================

function checkSurveyCompletion() {
    const requiredFields = ['overall_satisfaction', 'recommendation'];
    let allCompleted = true;
    
    requiredFields.forEach(fieldName => {
        const field = document.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]:checked`);
        if (!field) {
            allCompleted = false;
        }
    });
    
    document.getElementById('surveySubmitBtn').disabled = !allCompleted;
}

// ?¬ìš©??ID ?ì„±
function generateUserId() {
    return 'user_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
}

// ê²°ê³¼ ?¤ìš´ë¡œë“œ ?¨ìˆ˜
function downloadResults() {
    const completeData = {
        testInfo: {
            programName: "ASTER ë§¤ë ¥ ?êµ¬ ?„ë¡œê·¸ë¨",
            completedAt: new Date().toLocaleString('ko-KR'),
            userId: localStorage.getItem('userId') || 'anonymous'
        },
        selectedCategories: testSystem.stage1_selections,
        situationResponses: testSystem.stage2_situation_responses,
        personalityResponses: testSystem.stage2_personality_responses,
        reflectionResponses: testSystem.stage3_responses
    };
    
    const dataStr = JSON.stringify(completeData, null, 2);
    const dataBlob = new Blob([dataStr], {type: 'application/json'});
    
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = URL.createObjectURL(dataBlob);
    link.download = `ASTER_ê²°ê³¼_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json`;
    link.click();
}

}

// ê¸°ì¡´ ì½”ë“œ ë§ˆì?ë§?ë¶€ë¶„ì— ???¨ìˆ˜ë¥?ì¶”ê??˜ì„¸??

/**
 * '?ˆì‹œ ë³´ê¸°' ë²„íŠ¼???Œë????? ?µë? ?ˆì‹œ ëª©ë¡??ë³´ì—¬ì£¼ê±°???¨ê¸°???¨ìˆ˜
 * @param {HTMLElement} button - ?´ë¦­??ë²„íŠ¼ ?”ì†Œ
 * @param {number} questionId - ?„ì¬ ì§ˆë¬¸ ê·¸ë£¹??ID
 * @param {number} subIndex - ?„ì¬ ?˜ìœ„ ì§ˆë¬¸???¸ë±?? */
function toggleExamples(button, questionId, subIndex) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`exampleContainer_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    if (!container) return;

    const isVisible = container.classList.contains('visible');

    if (isVisible) {
        // ?´ë? ë³´ì¼ ??-> ?¨ê¸°ê¸?        container.classList.remove('visible');
        button.innerHTML = '?’¡ ?ˆì‹œ ë³´ê¸°';
    } else {
        // ?¨ê²¨???ˆì„ ??-> ë³´ì´ê¸?        const allQuestions = testSystem.getReflectionQuestions();
        const question = allQuestions.find(q => q.id === questionId);
    
        if (!question || !question.examples || !question.examples[subIndex]) {
            alert('??ì§ˆë¬¸???€???ˆì‹œê°€ ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.');
            return;
        }

        const examples = question.examples[subIndex];

        // ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆ ?´ìš© ì±„ìš°ê¸?        let contentHTML = '<div class="example-title">?’¬ ?´ëŸ° ?ìœ¼ë¡??µë??´ë³¼ ???ˆì–´??</div>';
        examples.forEach(example => {
            // "?ˆì‹œ 1: " ê°™ì? ë¶€ë¶„ì„ ?œê±°?˜ê³  ?´ìš©ë§?ì¶”ì¶œ
            const cleanExample = example.replace(/^?ˆì‹œ \d+: "/, '').replace(/"$/, '');
            contentHTML += `<div class="example-item">${cleanExample}</div>`;
        });
        container.innerHTML = contentHTML;

        // .visible ?´ë˜?¤ë? ì¶”ê??˜ì—¬ CSS ? ë‹ˆë©”ì´???¤í–‰
        container.classList.add('visible');
        button.innerHTML = '?’¡ ?ˆì‹œ ?«ê¸°';
    }
}

// ëª¨ë‹¬ ?«ê¸° ?¨ìˆ˜ (?¹ì‹œ ?†ë‹¤ë©?ì¶”ê?)
function closeModal(modalId) {
    const modal = document.getElementById(modalId);
    if (modal) {
        modal.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

// ëª¨ë‹¬ ?¸ë? ?´ë¦­???«ê¸° (ê¸°ì¡´ ?¨ìˆ˜ ?…ë°?´íŠ¸)
window.onclick = function(event) {
    const modals = ['exampleModal', 'templateModal', 'attractionModal'];
    modals.forEach(modalId => {
        const modal = document.getElementById(modalId);
        if (event.target === modal) {
            modal.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
}

/**
 * 'ê¸¸ì¡??ì§ˆë¬¸' ë²„íŠ¼???Œë????? ì§ˆë¬¸ ëª©ë¡??ë³´ì—¬ì£¼ê±°???¨ê¸°???¨ìˆ˜
 * @param {HTMLElement} button - ?´ë¦­??ë²„íŠ¼ ?”ì†Œ
 * @param {number} questionId - ?„ì¬ ì§ˆë¬¸ ê·¸ë£¹??ID
 * @param {number} subIndex - ?„ì¬ ?˜ìœ„ ì§ˆë¬¸???¸ë±?? */
function toggleGuideQuestions(button, questionId, subIndex) {
    // 1. ê¸¸ì¡??ì§ˆë¬¸???¤ì–´ê°?ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆ ?”ì†Œë¥?ì°¾ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.
    const container = document.getElementById(`guideQuestionsContainer_${questionId}_${subIndex}`);
    if (!container) return; // ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆê°€ ?†ìœ¼ë©??¨ìˆ˜ ì¢…ë£Œ

    // 2. ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆê°€ ?„ì¬ ?”ë©´??ë³´ì´???íƒœ?¸ì? ?•ì¸?©ë‹ˆ??
    const isVisible = container.classList.contains('visible');

    if (isVisible) {
        // 3-1. ë§Œì•½ ë³´ì´ê³??ˆë‹¤ë©? 'visible' ?´ë˜?¤ë? ?œê±°?˜ì—¬ CSS ? ë‹ˆë©”ì´?˜ìœ¼ë¡??¨ê¹?ˆë‹¤.
        container.classList.remove('visible');
        button.innerHTML = '?“ ê¸¸ì¡??ì§ˆë¬¸'; // ë²„íŠ¼ ?ìŠ¤?¸ë? ?ë˜?€ë¡??˜ëŒë¦½ë‹ˆ??
    } else {
        // 3-2. ë§Œì•½ ?¨ê²¨???ˆë‹¤ë©?
        // TEMPLATE_DATA?ì„œ ?„ì¬ ì§ˆë¬¸??ë§ëŠ” ê¸¸ì¡??ì§ˆë¬¸ ëª©ë¡??ê°€?¸ì˜µ?ˆë‹¤.
        const templates = TEMPLATE_DATA[questionId]?.[subIndex];
        if (!templates) {
            alert('??ì§ˆë¬¸???€??ê¸¸ì¡?´ê? ?†ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.');
            return;
        }

        // ê¸¸ì¡??ì§ˆë¬¸ ëª©ë¡??HTMLë¡?ë§Œë“­?ˆë‹¤.
        let contentHTML = '<div class="guide-title">?’¡ ?„ë˜ ì§ˆë¬¸?¤ì„ ê¸¸ì¡???¼ì•„ ?µë????ìœ ë¡?²Œ ?‘ì„±?´ë³´?¸ìš”!</div><ul>';
        templates.forEach(q => {
            contentHTML += `<li>${q}</li>`;
        });
        contentHTML += '</ul>';
        
        // ì»¨í…Œ?´ë„ˆ ?ˆì— ë§Œë“¤?´ì§„ HTML??ì±„ì›Œ?£ìŠµ?ˆë‹¤.
        container.innerHTML = contentHTML;

        // 'visible' ?´ë˜?¤ë? ì¶”ê??˜ì—¬ CSS ? ë‹ˆë©”ì´?˜ìœ¼ë¡?ë¶€?œëŸ½ê²??¼ì¹©?ˆë‹¤.
        container.classList.add('visible');
        button.innerHTML = '?“ ê¸¸ì¡??ì§ˆë¬¸ ?«ê¸°'; // ë²„íŠ¼ ?ìŠ¤?¸ë? '?«ê¸°'ë¡?ë°”ê¿‰?ˆë‹¤.
    }
}

// ==================== ë§¤ë ¥ ?¤ì›Œ???œìŠ¤??(?„ì „ ??ë²„ì „) ====================
